	y = 1

					rule = TBK_ai_behavior
					option = WALLNUT_HARMONY
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TBK_ai_behavior

				}

					rule = TBK_ai_behavior

				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TBK_ai_behavior

				}

	icon = GFX_goal_constitutional_guarantees
	cost = 7
	relative_position_id = TBK_entry_world_stage
	prerequisite = { focus = TBK_entry_world_stage }
	x = 0
	y = 1
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	available = {
		CTH = {
			exists = yes
			has_war = no
			OR = {
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = neutrality
				has_government = democratic
			}
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = TBK
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
    	factor = 10
    }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TBK_colthage_treaty"
		custom_effect_tooltip = TBK_if_accepts_colthage_relations_tp
		effect_tooltip = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = CTH
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CTH
				modifier = TBK_improved_relations
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { 
				target = CTH
				modifier = trade_treaty 
			}
			CTH = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TBK
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = TBK
					modifier = TBK_improved_relations
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { 
					target = TBK
					modifier = trade_treaty 
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CTH = { country_event = { id = tobuck_vasile.17 } }
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = TBK_fighter_sales
	icon = GFX_goal_phoenix_plane
	cost = 7
	relative_position_id = TBK_back_to_gunrunning
	prerequisite = { focus = TBK_back_to_gunrunning }
	x = 2
	y = 1
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	available = {
		692 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
    	factor = 10
    }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TBK_fighter_sales"
		custom_effect_tooltip = TBK_vasile_unlock_fighter_sales_tp
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = fighter_bonus
			bonus = 1.0
			uses = 1
			category = light_fighter
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				has_tech = iw_small_airframe
			}
			set_technology = {
				aa_lmg = 1
				engines_1 = 1
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fighter_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = light_air
			}
			generic_early_fighter = yes
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe_1
				variant_name = "Early Fighter"
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				NOT = {
					has_tech = iw_small_airframe
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
				iw_small_airframe = 1
				aa_lmg = 1
				engines_1 = 1
			}
			generic_early_fighter = yes
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe_1
				variant_name = "Early Fighter"
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = early_fighter
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fighter_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				category = light_fighter
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				early_fighter = 1
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_airframe
				amount = 50
			}
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = TBK_tobuck_bell
	icon = GFX_goal_TBK_taco
	cost = 7
	relative_position_id = TBK_domestic_civilian_monopoly
	prerequisite = { focus = TBK_domestic_civilian_monopoly }
	x = -1
	y = 1
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	ai_will_do = {
    	factor = 10
    }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TBK_tobuck_bell"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_radio
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_radio
				add_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_bell_radio
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_mages
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_mages
				add_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_bell_mages
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_radio_mages
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_radio_mages
				add_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_combined
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies
				add_idea = TBK_vasile_domestic_companies_bell
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {

shared_focus = {
	id = TBK_claim_warzena
	icon = GFX_goal_ideology_monarchist
	cost = 5
	relative_position_id = TBK_warzenan_loyalists
	prerequisite = { focus = TBK_warzenan_loyalists }
	prerequisite = { focus = TBK_tobuckian_levies }
	x = 1
	y = 1
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	will_lead_to_war_with = WAR
	ai_will_do = {
    	factor = 10
    }
	available = {
		is_subject = no
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TBK_claim_warzena"
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WAR
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					OR = {
						has_guaranteed = WAR
						is_in_faction_with = WAR
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TBK_explain_warzena_war_timer_tp
			hidden_effect = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_guaranteed = WAR
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = WAR
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = WAR
					}
					country_event = { id = tobuck_baragzen.10 }
				}
				WAR = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction = yes
						}
						country_event = { id = tobuck_baragzen.9 }
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = TBK_confusing_war
							days = 180
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							TBK = {
								has_completed_focus = TBK_clandestine_movement
							}
						}
						add_ideas = TBK_warzena_secret_revolt
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							TBK = {
								has_completed_focus = TBK_open_movement
							}
						}
						add_ideas = TBK_warzena_open_revolt
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = { 
					type = annex_everything 
					target = WAR
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = WAR
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				create_wargoal = { 
					type = annex_everything 
					target = WAR
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = WAR
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
					create_wargoal = {
						target = CDR
						type = annex_everything
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = CDR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						BKH = {
							exists = yes
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					create_wargoal = {
						target = BKH
						type = annex_everything
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = BKH
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				CGI = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes }
				CDR = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes }
				BKH = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes }
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

				}

				}

					}

				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_3
					amount = 25
					producer = TBK
					variant_name = "Advanced Fighter"
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = improved_small_airframe
					has_tech = engines_3
					has_tech = aa_hmg
				}

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Improved Fighter"
					type = small_plane_airframe_2
					modules = {
						fixed_main_weapon_slot = heavy_mg_2x
						engine_type_slot = engine_3_1x
						special_type_slot_1 = lmg_defense_turret
					}

shared_focus = {
	id = TBK_navy_final
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_navy_doctrines_tactics
	cost = 7
	relative_position_id = TBK_battleship_designs
	prerequisite = { focus = TBK_battleship_designs }
	prerequisite = { focus = TBK_cruiser_design }
	x = 1
	y = 1
	available_if_capitulated = yes
	ai_will_do = {
    	factor = 3
    }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus TBK_navy_final"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TBK_cruiser_navy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TBK_cruiser_navy
				add_idea = TBK_cruiser_navy_final
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TBK_sub_navy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TBK_sub_navy
				add_idea = TBK_sub_navy_final
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TBK_air_force_final_tp
		}
	}
}
